NN architecture:

Four 4*13 matrix
Two 1*4 matrix

x_train_RL = {'order': [], 'players': [], 'hand': [], 'bets': [], 'tricks': [], 'lead': []}

order -> 4 * 13 Matrix. 1-52 numbers filled. represents which card is played by which player.
players -> 4 * 13 Matrix. initially filled with zeros.
hand -> hand card of a player. thrown card replaced with 0. 1 means current remaining card.
bets -> bets of each player.
tricks -> similar to table cards.
lead -> highest cards like Ace.
